(function () {
  var suppressionFlagKey = "__OPGG_SUPPRESS_GA_ADS__";
  var clientRulesKey = "__OPGG_AD_SUPPRESS_CLIENT_RULES__";
  var cookieName = "_sp";
  var cookieDomain = ".op.gg";
  var cookieValue = "1";
  var gaId = "G-HKZFKE5JEL";
  var gtmId = "GTM-WKTM6W8T";
  var supportedConditionKeys = ["absentCookieNames","devicePixelRatio","nonUserAgentPattern","pathPrefixes","referrer","requiredLanguagePrefixes","screen","userAgentPattern","viewport"];
  var loadedKey = '__OPGG_GOOGLE_ANALYTICS_GATE_LOADED__';

  function ensureGoogleQueue() {
    window.dataLayer = window.dataLayer || [];
    window.gtag = window.gtag || function () { window.dataLayer.push(arguments); };
  }

  function appendScript(id, src, attrs) {
    if (document.getElementById(id)) {
      return;
    }

    var script = document.createElement('script');
    script.id = id;
    script.src = src;
    script.async = true;

    if (attrs) {
      Object.keys(attrs).forEach(function (key) {
        script.setAttribute(key, attrs[key]);
      });
    }

    (document.head || document.documentElement).appendChild(script);
  }

  function loadGoogleAnalytics() {
    if (window[loadedKey]) {
      return;
    }

    window[loadedKey] = true;
    ensureGoogleQueue();

    window.dataLayer.push({ 'gtm.start': new Date().getTime(), event: 'gtm.js' });
    appendScript('_next-gtm', 'https://www.googletagmanager.com/gtm.js?id=' + encodeURIComponent(gtmId), {
      'data-ntpc': 'GTM',
    });

    window.gtag('js', new Date());
    window.gtag('config', gaId);
    appendScript('_next-ga', 'https://www.googletagmanager.com/gtag/js?id=' + encodeURIComponent(gaId));
  }

  function inRange(value, min, max) {
    if (typeof min === 'number' && value < min) {
      return false;
    }
    if (typeof max === 'number' && value > max) {
      return false;
    }
    return true;
  }

  function hasCookie(cookieString, name) {
    return cookieString.split(';').some(function (cookie) {
      return cookie.trim().indexOf(name + '=') === 0;
    });
  }

  function matchesLanguagePrefixes(languages, prefixes) {
    if (!Array.isArray(prefixes) || prefixes.length === 0) {
      return true;
    }

    return languages.some(function (language) {
      var normalizedLanguage = String(language || '').trim().toLowerCase();

      return prefixes.some(function (prefix) {
        return normalizedLanguage.indexOf(prefix) === 0;
      });
    });
  }

  function matchesPattern(value, pattern) {
    try {
      return new RegExp(pattern).test(value);
    } catch (error) {
      return false;
    }
  }

  function matchesPathPrefixes(pathname, pathPrefixes) {
    if (!Array.isArray(pathPrefixes)) {
      return true;
    }

    var normalizedPathname = String(pathname || '').replace(/\/+$/, '') || '/';
    normalizedPathname = normalizedPathname.replace(
      /^\/(?:en|ko|ja|pl|fr|de|es|nl|da|sv|no|ru|hu|fi|tr|ro|pt|zh-cn|zh-tw|ar|sr|it|th|vi)(?=\/|$)/i,
      '',
    ) || '/';

    return pathPrefixes.some(function (pathPrefix) {
      return normalizedPathname === pathPrefix || normalizedPathname.indexOf(pathPrefix + '/') === 0;
    });
  }

  function hasOnlySupportedConditionKeys(conditions) {
    return Object.keys(conditions).every(function (key) {
      return supportedConditionKeys.indexOf(key) >= 0;
    });
  }

  function matchesRule(rule) {
    var conditions = rule && rule.clientConditions;
    if (!conditions) {
      return false;
    }
    if (!hasOnlySupportedConditionKeys(conditions)) {
      return false;
    }

    if (!matchesPathPrefixes(window.location && window.location.pathname, conditions.pathPrefixes)) {
      return false;
    }

    if (conditions.viewport) {
      if (
        !inRange(window.innerWidth, conditions.viewport.minWidth, conditions.viewport.maxWidth) ||
        !inRange(window.innerHeight, conditions.viewport.minHeight, conditions.viewport.maxHeight)
      ) {
        return false;
      }
    }

    if (conditions.screen) {
      if (
        !inRange(window.screen && window.screen.width ? window.screen.width : 0, conditions.screen.minWidth, conditions.screen.maxWidth) ||
        !inRange(window.screen && window.screen.height ? window.screen.height : 0, conditions.screen.minHeight, conditions.screen.maxHeight)
      ) {
        return false;
      }
    }

    if (conditions.devicePixelRatio && !inRange(window.devicePixelRatio || 1, conditions.devicePixelRatio.min, conditions.devicePixelRatio.max)) {
      return false;
    }
    if (conditions.referrer && conditions.referrer.absent && document.referrer) {
      return false;
    }

    var languages = [];
    if (Array.isArray(window.navigator && window.navigator.languages)) {
      languages = languages.concat(window.navigator.languages);
    }
    if (window.navigator && window.navigator.language) {
      languages.push(window.navigator.language);
    }
    if (!matchesLanguagePrefixes(languages, conditions.requiredLanguagePrefixes)) {
      return false;
    }

    var userAgent = (window.navigator && window.navigator.userAgent) || '';
    if (conditions.userAgentPattern && !matchesPattern(userAgent, conditions.userAgentPattern)) {
      return false;
    }
    if (conditions.nonUserAgentPattern && matchesPattern(userAgent, conditions.nonUserAgentPattern)) {
      return false;
    }

    var cookieString = document.cookie || '';
    var absentCookieNames = Array.isArray(conditions.absentCookieNames) ? conditions.absentCookieNames : [];
    for (var i = 0; i < absentCookieNames.length; i += 1) {
      if (hasCookie(cookieString, absentCookieNames[i])) {
        return false;
      }
    }

    return true;
  }

  function writeSuppressionCookie(maxAge) {
    var cookieParts = [cookieName + '=' + cookieValue, 'Max-Age=' + maxAge, 'Path=/', 'SameSite=Lax'];
    if (window.location.hostname === 'op.gg' || window.location.hostname.slice(-6) === '.op.gg') {
      cookieParts.push('Domain=' + cookieDomain);
    }
    if (window.location.protocol === 'https:') {
      cookieParts.push('Secure');
    }
    document.cookie = cookieParts.join('; ');
  }

  try {
    if (window[suppressionFlagKey]) {
      return;
    }

    var rules = window[clientRulesKey];
    if (!Array.isArray(rules) || rules.length === 0) {
      loadGoogleAnalytics();
      return;
    }

    for (var i = 0; i < rules.length; i += 1) {
      if (matchesRule(rules[i])) {
        window[suppressionFlagKey] = true;
        writeSuppressionCookie(rules[i].rememberForSeconds);
        return;
      }
    }

    loadGoogleAnalytics();
  } catch (error) {
    loadGoogleAnalytics();
  }
